{\\n167: public:\\n168:   /**\\n169:    * Return a sorted vector of registered factory names.\\n170:    */\\n171:   static std::vector<absl::string_view> registeredNames(bool include_disabled = false) {\\n172:     std::vector<absl::string_view> ret;\\n173: \\n174:     ret.reserve(factories().size());\\n175: \\n176:     for (const auto& [factory_name, factory] : factories()) {\\n177:       if \\n495: /**\\n496:  * Factory registration template. Enables users to register a particular implementation factory with\\n497:  * the FactoryRegistry by instantiating this templated class with the specific factory class and the\\n498:  * general Base class to which that factory conforms.\\n499:  *\\n500:  * Because factories are generally registered once and live for the length of the program, the\\n501:  * standard use of this class is static instantiation within a linked implementation's translation\\n502:  * unit. FactoryRegistry<Base>::registerFactory(instance_, instance_.name());\\n535:     } else {\\n536:       ASSERT(deprecated_names.size() != 0,\\n537:              \\\"Attempted to register a factory without a name or deprecated name\\\");\\n538:     }\\n539: \\n540:     for (auto deprecated_name : deprecated_names) {\\n541:       ASSERT(!deprecated_name.empty());\\n542: \\n495: /**\\n496:  * Factory registration template. Enables users to register a particular implementation factory with\\n497:  * the FactoryRegistry by instantiating this templated class with the specific factory class and the\\n498:  * general Base class to which that factory conforms.\\n499:  *\\n500:  * Because factories are generally registered once and live for the length of the program, the\\n501:  * standard use of this class is static instantiation within a linked implementation's translation\\n502:  * unit. This means that we have to ignore\\n520:     // multiple attempts to register the same category and can't detect\\n521:     // duplicate categories.\\n522:     if (!FactoryCategoryRegistry::isRegistered(instance_.category())) {\\n523:       FactoryCategoryRegistry::registerCategory(instance_.category(),\\n524:                                                 new FactoryRegistryProxyImpl<Base>());\\n525:     }\\n526:   }\\n527: \\n528:   /**\\n529:    * Constructor that registers an instance of the factory with the FactoryRegistry along with\\n530:    * deprecated names.\\n531:    */\\n532:   explicit RegisterFactory(std::initializer_list<absl::string_view> deprecated_names) {\\n533:     if (!instance_.name().empty()) {\\n534:       FactoryRegistry<Base>::registerFactory(instance_, instance_.name());\\n535:     } else {\\n536:       ASSERT(deprecated_names.size() != 0,\\n537:              \\\"Attempted to register a factory without a name or deprecated name\\\");\\n538:     }\\n539: \\n540:     for (auto deprecated_name : deprecated_names) {\\n541:       ASSERT(!deprecated_name.empty());\\n542:       FactoryRegistry<Base>::registerFactory(instance_, deprecated_name, instance_.name());\\n543:     }\\n544: \\n545:     if (!FactoryCategoryRegistry::isRegistered(instance_.category())) {\\n546:       FactoryCategoryRegistry::registerCategory(instance_.category(),\\n547:                                                 new FactoryRegistryProxyImpl<Base>());\\n548:     }\\n549:   }\\n550: \\n551: \\n559:   /**\\n560:    * Constructor that registers an instance of the factory with the FactoryRegistry along with\\n561:    * vendor specific version and deprecated names.\\n562:    */\\n563: instantiation of extensions. Here is the comprehensive architecture:\\n\\n## Core Registry Pattern\\n\\nThe main registry implementation is in `envoy/registry/registry.h`, which contains three key template classes:\\n\\n1. **FactoryRegistry<Base>**: A static template class that maintains a registry of factories for a given base factory type. It implements:\\n   - `factories()`: Returns the static map of registered factories\\n   - `registerFactory()`: Registers a factory instance with a given name\\n   - `getFactory()`: Retrieves a factory by name\\n   - `registeredNames()`: Lists all registered factory names\\n   - `versionedFactories()`: Stores vendor-specific version information\\n   - `factoriesByType()`: Maps configuration message types to factories\\n   - `disableFactory()`: Disables a factory by name\\n\\n2. **RegisterFactory<T, Base>**: A template class used to register a factory at static initialization time. Its constructor automatically registers an instance of template parameter T with the FactoryRegistry<Base>. When instantiated statically, it causes the factory to self-register during program startup.\\n\\n3. **FactoryCategoryRegistry**: A static registry that groups factories by category (e.g., \\\"envoy.filters.listener\\\", \\\"envoy.access_logs\\\"), enabling discovery of all factories within a category.\\n\\n## Static Extension Registration\\n\\nExtensions self-register at static initialization time using two macros defined in `envoy/registry/registry.h`:\\n\\n- **REGISTER_FACTORY(FactoryClass, BaseFactoryClass)**: Creates a static instance of RegisterFactory<FactoryClass, BaseFactoryClass>, causing automatic registration during program initialization.\\n- **LEGACY_REGISTER_FACTORY(FactoryClass, BaseFactoryClass, DeprecatedName)**: Registers a factory with deprecated name support for backwards compatibility.\\n\\nThese macros are used throughout the codebase in config.cc files (e.g., `source/extensions/filters/http/wasm/config.cc`, `source/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/config.cc`), where each extension implementation creates a static factory registration.\\n\\n## Base Factory Architecture\\n\\nAll extensions inherit from factory base classes defined in `envoy/config/typed_config.h`:\\n\\n- **UntypedFactory**: Base class requiring `name()`, `category()`, and optional `configTypes()` methods.\\n- **TypedFactory**: Extends UntypedFactory, requiring `createEmptyConfigProto()` to support type-safe configuration validation.\\n\\nSpecialized factory base classes for different extension types include:\\n- `ClusterFactory` in `envoy/upstream/cluster_factory.h`\\n- `NamedListenerFilterConfigFactory`, `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` in `envoy/server/filter_config.h`\\n- `AccessLogInstanceFactory` in `envoy/access_log/access_log_config.h`\\n- `TracerFactory` in `envoy/server/tracer_config.h`\\n- `TypedMetadataFactory` in `envoy/config/typed_metadata.h`\\n\\n## Factory Instantiation and Lookup\\n\\nThe `source/common/config/utility.h` file provides utility functions for factory discovery:\\n\\n- `Utility::getFactoryByName<Factory>(name)`: Looks up a factory by name, returns nullptr if not found\\n- `Utility::getAndCheckFactoryByName<Factory>(name)`: Looks up by name with error checking\\n- `Utility::getFactory<Factory, ProtoMessage>(message)`: Looks up by type URL or name\\n- `Utility::getAndCheckFactory<Factory, ProtoMessage>(message)`: Type-safe factory lookup with validation\\n\\nThese functions internally call `Registry::FactoryRegistry<Factory>::getFactory(name)` to retrieve the registered factory instance.\\n\\n## Template Factory Bases\\n\\nCommon extension patterns use template base classes for consistent implementation:\\n- `source/extensions/tracers/common/factory_base.h`: FactoryBase<ConfigProto> template for tracer factories\\n- `source/extensions/compression/common/compressor/factory_base.h`: CompressorLibraryFactoryBase template\\n- `source/extensions/filters/network/thrift_proxy/filters/factory_base.h`: FactoryBase<ConfigProto> for Thrift filters\\n- `source/extensions/filters/network/dubbo_proxy/filters/factory_base.h`: FactoryBase<ConfigProto> for Dubbo filters\\n\\n## Test Infrastructure\\n\\nTest utilities in `test/test_common/registry.h` provide:\\n- **InjectFactory<Base>**: Test helper that injects a mock factory and restores the original on destruction\\n- **InjectFactoryCategory<Base>**: Test helper for registering factory categories in tests\\n\\nThe test file `test/common/config/registry_test.cc` demonstrates:\\n- Registration of test factories using REGISTER_FACTORY\\n- Verification that factories are discoverable by name and category\\n- Support for versioned factories with version metadata\\n- Proper isolation and restoration of factory registrations in tests\\n\\n## Extension Discovery and Validation\\n\\nThe file `test/exe/check_extensions_against_registry_test.cc` shows how the system discovers all registered extensions through `FactoryCategoryRegistry::registeredFactories()` and validates that extension configuration types match those declared in the registry.\\n\\nThis design achieves loose coupling between Envoy core and extensions, allowing extensions to be compiled into the binary and discovered at runtime through the registry, with support for versioning, deprecation, and type-safe configuration.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1342,"cache_read_input_tokens":84588,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1342},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"571eca37-fee2-4fd0-a35a-58c008347fbc","uuid":"bbf903fa-4030-43cf-bce0-b087df8bf41c"}

instantiation of extensions. Here is the comprehensive architecture:\\n\\n## Core Registry Pattern\\n\\nThe main registry implementation is in `envoy/registry/registry.h`, which contains three key template classes:\\n\\n1. **FactoryRegistry<Base>**: A static template class that maintains a registry of factories for a given base factory type. It implements:\\n   - `factories()`: Returns the static map of registered factories\\n   - `registerFactory()`: Registers a factory instance with a given name\\n   - `getFactory()`: Retrieves a factory by name\\n   - `registeredNames()`: Lists all registered factory names\\n   - `versionedFactories()`: Stores vendor-specific version information\\n   - `factoriesByType()`: Maps configuration message types to factories\\n   - `disableFactory()`: Disables a factory by name\\n\\n2. **RegisterFactory<T, Base>**: A template class used to register a factory at static initialization time. Its constructor automatically registers an instance of template parameter T with the FactoryRegistry<Base>. When instantiated statically, it causes the factory to self-register during program startup.\\n\\n3. **FactoryCategoryRegistry**: A static registry that groups factories by category (e.g., \\\"envoy.filters.listener\\\", \\\"envoy.access_logs\\\"), enabling discovery of all factories within a category.\\n\\n## Static Extension Registration\\n\\nExtensions self-register at static initialization time using two macros defined in `envoy/registry/registry.h`:\\n\\n- **REGISTER_FACTORY(FactoryClass, BaseFactoryClass)**: Creates a static instance of RegisterFactory<FactoryClass, BaseFactoryClass>, causing automatic registration during program initialization.\\n- **LEGACY_REGISTER_FACTORY(FactoryClass, BaseFactoryClass, DeprecatedName)**: Registers a factory with deprecated name support for backwards compatibility.\\n\\nThese macros are used throughout the codebase in config.cc files (e.g., `source/extensions/filters/http/wasm/config.cc`, `source/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/config.cc`), where each extension implementation creates a static factory registration.\\n\\n## Base Factory Architecture\\n\\nAll extensions inherit from factory base classes defined in `envoy/config/typed_config.h`:\\n\\n- **UntypedFactory**: Base class requiring `name()`, `category()`, and optional `configTypes()` methods.\\n- **TypedFactory**: Extends UntypedFactory, requiring `createEmptyConfigProto()` to support type-safe configuration validation.\\n\\nSpecialized factory base classes for different extension types include:\\n- `ClusterFactory` in `envoy/upstream/cluster_factory.h`\\n- `NamedListenerFilterConfigFactory`, `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` in `envoy/server/filter_config.h`\\n- `AccessLogInstanceFactory` in `envoy/access_log/access_log_config.h`\\n- `TracerFactory` in `envoy/server/tracer_config.h`\\n- `TypedMetadataFactory` in `envoy/config/typed_metadata.h`\\n\\n## Factory Instantiation and Lookup\\n\\nThe `source/common/config/utility.h` file provides utility functions for factory discovery:\\n\\n- `Utility::getFactoryByName<Factory>(name)`: Looks up a factory by name, returns nullptr if not found\\n- `Utility::getAndCheckFactoryByName<Factory>(name)`: Looks up by name with error checking\\n- `Utility::getFactory<Factory, ProtoMessage>(message)`: Looks up by type URL or name\\n- `Utility::getAndCheckFactory<Factory, ProtoMessage>(message)`: Type-safe factory lookup with validation\\n\\nThese functions internally call `Registry::FactoryRegistry<Factory>::getFactory(name)` to retrieve the registered factory instance.\\n\\n## Template Factory Bases\\n\\nCommon extension patterns use template base classes for consistent implementation:\\n- `source/extensions/tracers/common/factory_base.h`: FactoryBase<ConfigProto> template for tracer factories\\n- `source/extensions/compression/common/compressor/factory_base.h`: CompressorLibraryFactoryBase template\\n- `source/extensions/filters/network/thrift_proxy/filters/factory_base.h`: FactoryBase<ConfigProto> for Thrift filters\\n- `source/extensions/filters/network/dubbo_proxy/filters/factory_base.h`: FactoryBase<ConfigProto> for Dubbo filters\\n\\n## Test Infrastructure\\n\\nTest utilities in `test/test_common/registry.h` provide:\\n- **InjectFactory<Base>**: Test helper that injects a mock factory and restores the original on destruction\\n- **InjectFactoryCategory<Base>**: Test helper for registering factory categories in tests\\n\\nThe test file `test/common/config/registry_test.cc` demonstrates:\\n- Registration of test factories using REGISTER_FACTORY\\n- Verification that factories are discoverable by name and category\\n- Support for versioned factories with version metadata\\n- Proper isolation and restoration of factory registrations in tests\\n\\n## Extension Discovery and Validation\\n\\nThe file `test/exe/check_extensions_against_registry_test.cc` shows how the system discovers all registered extensions through `FactoryCategoryRegistry::registeredFactories()` and validates that extension configuration types match those declared in the registry.\\n\\nThis design achieves loose coupling between Envoy core and extensions, allowing extensions to be compiled into the binary and discovered at runtime through the registry, with support for versioning, deprecation, and type-safe configuration.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
